function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.110!');
}

	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') != '23d3191a98af3c9ca666a0420795afafae6acae7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '23d3191a98af3c9ca666a0420795afafae6acae7') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '1992a7c3251894adc180ccc17d22229d3857a58f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '23d3191a98af3c9ca666a0420795afafae6acae7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != 'c1825bd188c34988cd4eee188794b9c0d5e0bf4f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'c1825bd188c34988cd4eee188794b9c0d5e0bf4f') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '2a7acac06b6258cfdfe951117063f1554b7b3450') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'c1825bd188c34988cd4eee188794b9c0d5e0bf4f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('index_desktop.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index_desktop.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('index_desktop.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index_desktop.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index_desktop.php') != '3cf763fff25eaa88e38434798e5c7c4878baeeae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index_desktop.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index_desktop.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index_desktop.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index_desktop.php') !== '3cf763fff25eaa88e38434798e5c7c4878baeeae') {
		if (@sha1_file('index_desktop.php') !== '70075f2ae88c2109d4bafe93c2f033b4aef8ccb9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index_desktop.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index_desktop.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index_desktop.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index_desktop.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('index_desktop.php') !== '3cf763fff25eaa88e38434798e5c7c4878baeeae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index_desktop.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index_mobile.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index_mobile.php');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('index_mobile.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index_mobile.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index_mobile.php') != '229f4c1c350c0c7c5c707b4751962a370314b2ed') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index_mobile.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index_mobile.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index_mobile.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '229f4c1c350c0c7c5c707b4751962a370314b2ed') {
		if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== 'e347c771cafee2c184421c3da1ced990453127c6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index_mobile.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index_mobile.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index_mobile.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index_mobile.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '229f4c1c350c0c7c5c707b4751962a370314b2ed') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index_mobile.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') != '64614a9e35f4b8225f74ca271c271133b84c3850') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '64614a9e35f4b8225f74ca271c271133b84c3850') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '94881e49fdb2110826329a68ee3263934a6c3309') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '64614a9e35f4b8225f74ca271c271133b84c3850') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
		}
	}
}
